[SNT] ingredient course [  /SNT]   Input: ['[TRIPLE] The_Eiffel_Tower height 324_meters  [TRIPLE] The_Eiffel_Tower built_in 1889  [TRIPLE] The_Eiffel_Tower architect Gustave_Eiffel']  Output: [SNT] height built_in architect  The Eiffel Tower is a wrought-iron lattice tower located on the Champ de Mars in Paris, France. It was named after the engineer Gustave Eiffel, whose company designed and built the tower. Constructed from 1887 to 1889 as an entrance to the 1889 World's Fair, it was initially criticized by some of France's leading artists and intellectuals for its design, but it has become a global cultural icon of France and one of the most recognizable structures in the world. The Eiffel Tower is the most-visited paid monument in the world; 6.91 million people ascended it in 2015. The tower is 324 meters (1,063 ft) tall, about the same height as an 81-story building, and the highest structure in Paris. It was the tallest man-made structure in the

It follows the pattern of subject, predicate, object (SPO) triplets. Each triplet consists of a subject, a predicate, and an object. The subject is the entity being described, the predicate is the relationship or property being described, and the object is the value or fact associated with the subject and predicate. In this case, the subjects are entities such as Elliot, AlmaMater University of Texas at Austin, Sandesh, Turkey, Azerbaijan, Ampara Hospital, Apollo 12, Mumbai Harbor, the predicates are relationships such as See, affiliations, compete_in, mascot, deathPlace, leader, leaderTitle, dedicatedTo,

[SNT] material nativeName designer location dedicatedTo [  The SNT (Subject, Predicate, Object) format represents triples in RDF (Resource Description Framework), which is a standard model for data interchange on the web. Each triple consists of a subject, a predicate, and an object. The subject is the entity being described, the predicate is the relationship between the subject and the object, and the object is the value of the relationship. In the examples provided, the subjects are universities, dishes, cities, countries, leaders, and monuments; the predicates are relationships such as "affiliations," "compete_in," "mascot," "deathPlace," "leaderName," "dedicatedTo," and "location"; and the objects are values such as "University_of_Texas_System," "Big_12_Conference," "Hook_em_(mascot)," "St._Louis," "Francis_G._Slay," "Atatürk_Monument_(İzmir)," "Bronze," "French_language," "Istanbul," "Ankara," "Ahmet_Davutoğlu," "Azerbaijan," "Artur_Rasizade," "Eastern_Province,_Sri_Lanka," "Sri_Lanka," and "Austin
